### <a name="hive-queries-can-use-tez-in-hdinsight-31"></a><span data-ttu-id="79c73-1501">Hive 查詢可在 HDinsight 3.1 中使用 Tez</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1501">Hive queries can use Tez in HDInsight 3.1</span></span>

        set hive.execution.engine=tez;
        select sc_status, count(*), histogram_numeric(sc_bytes,5) from website_logs_orc_local group by sc_status;

<span data-ttu-id="79c73-1506">Hortonworks 在標準效能評比中，已發表一份關於 Hive 查詢搭配 Tez 而提升效能的詳細數據。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1506">Hortonworks has published a detailed breakdown of Hive query performance enhancements with Tez as delivered in standard benchmarks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1507">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [Apache Hive 13 for Enterprise Hadoop 效能評比](http://hortonworks.com/blog/benchmarking-apache-hive-13-enterprise-hadoop/)(英文)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1507">For details, see [Benchmarking Apache Hive 13 for Enterprise Hadoop](http://hortonworks.com/blog/benchmarking-apache-hive-13-enterprise-hadoop/).</span></span>

### <a name="dos--donts-between-cluster-versions"></a><span data-ttu-id="79c73-1513">叢集版本之間的注意事項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1513">Dos & Don'ts between cluster versions</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79c73-1514">**與 HDInsight 3.1 叢集搭配使用的 Oozie 中繼存放區與舊版的 HDInsight 2.1 叢集無法回溯相容，且兩者無法與此舊版本搭配使用**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1514">**Oozie metastores used with an HDInsight 3.1 cluster are not backward compatible with HDInsight 2.1 clusters, and they cannot be used with this previous version**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79c73-1515">與 HDInsight 3.1 叢集一起部署的自訂 Oozie metastore 資料庫，無法在 HDInsight 2.1 叢集上重複使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1515">A custom Oozie metastore database deployed with an HDInsight 3.1 cluster cannot be reused with an HDInsight 2.1 cluster.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1516">這是 hello 情況下，即使 hello 中繼存放區產生與 HDInsight 2.1 叢集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1516">This is hello case even if hello metastore originated with an HDInsight 2.1 cluster.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1517">不支援這種情況下，因為搭配 HDInsight 3.1 叢集，使它不再與 hello hello HDInsight 2.1 叢集所需的中繼存放區相容時，取得升級 hello 中繼存放區結構描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1517">This scenario is not supported because hello metastore schema gets upgraded when used with an  HDInsight 3.1 cluster, so it is no longer compatible with hello metastore required by hello HDInsight 2.1 clusters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1518">任何嘗試 tooreuse 搭配 HDInsight 3.1 叢集的 Oozie 中繼存放區會呈現無用 hello HDInsight 2.1 叢集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1518">Any attempt tooreuse an Oozie metastore that has been used with an HDInsight 3.1 cluster render hello HDInsight 2.1 cluster useless.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79c73-1519">**叢集之間無法共用 Oozie 中繼存放區。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1519">**Oozie metastores cannot be shared across clusters.**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79c73-1520">Oozie 中繼存放區是附加的 toospecific 群集，而不能在叢集中共用它們。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1520">Oozie metastores are attached toospecific clusters, and they cannot be shared across clusters.</span></span>

### <a name="breaking-changes"></a><span data-ttu-id="79c73-1521">重大變更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1521">Breaking changes</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="79c73-1522">**前置詞語法**： 只有 hello"wasb: / /"HDInsight 3.1 與 3.0 叢集中的支援語法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1522">**Prefix syntax**: Only hello "wasb://" syntax is supported in HDInsight 3.1 and 3.0 clusters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1523">較舊的 hello"asv: / /"語法支援 HDInsight 2.1 和 1.6 的叢集，但它不支援 HDInsight 3.1 或 3.0 的叢集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1523">hello older "asv://" syntax is supported in HDInsight 2.1 and 1.6 clusters, but it is not supported in HDInsight 3.1 or 3.0 clusters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1524">這表示任何工作提交 tooan HDInsight 3.1 或叢集的明確 3.0，會使用 「 hello 」 asv: / /"語法將會失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1524">This means that any jobs submitted tooan HDInsight 3.1  or 3.0 cluster that explicitly uses hello "asv://" syntax will fail.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1525">hello"wasb: / /"應該改為使用語法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1525">hello "wasb://" syntax should be used instead.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1526">此外，工作提交 tooany HDInsight 3.1 或 3.0 建立的叢集，其中包含現有中繼存放區與明確參考使用 hello tooresources"asv: / /"語法將會失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1526">Also, jobs submitted tooany HDInsight 3.1 or 3.0 clusters that are created with an existing metastore that contains explicit references tooresources using hello "asv://" syntax will fail.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1527">這些中繼存放區需要重建使用 hello toobe"wasb: / /"語法 tooaddress 資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1527">These metastores need toobe re-created using hello "wasb://" syntax tooaddress resources.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="79c73-1528">**連接埠**: hello hello HDInsight 服務所使用的連接埠已變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1528">**Ports**: hello ports used by hello HDInsight service have changed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1529">hello 連接埠號碼已使用了 hello Windows 作業系統的 hello 暫時連接埠範圍內。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1529">hello port numbers that were being used were within hello ephemeral port range of hello Windows operating system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1530">對於短期的網際網路通訊協定通訊，會自動從預設定義的暫時範圍中配置連接埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1530">Ports are allocated automatically from a predefined ephemeral range for short-lived Internet protocol-based communications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1531">hello 組新的 Hortonworks Data Platform (HDP) 允許的服務連接埠號碼會發生衝突時的 hello hello 前端節點上執行的服務所使用的連接埠可能會發生此範圍 tooavoid 之外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1531">hello new set of allowed Hortonworks Data Platform (HDP) service port numbers are outside this range tooavoid encountering conflicts that could arise with hello ports used by services running on hello head node.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1532">hello 新的連接埠號碼，應該不會造成任何重大變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1532">hello new port numbers should not cause any breaking changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1533">如下所示為 hello 所使用的數字：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1533">hello numbers used are as follows:</span></span>

## <a name="hortonworks-release-notes"></a><span data-ttu-id="79c73-1673">Hortonworks 版本資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1673">Hortonworks release notes</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1675">HDInsight 3.1 版會使用為基礎的 hello Hadoop 散發[Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.7][hdp-2-1-7]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1675">HDInsight version 3.1 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on hello [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.7][hdp-2-1-7].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1676">這是使用 2014 年 11 月 7 日之後的 hello Azure 入口網站時，建立 hello 預設 Hadoop 叢集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1676">This is hello default Hadoop cluster created when using hello Azure portal after 11/7/2014.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1677">2014 年 11 月 7 日依據 hello 之前建立的 HDInsight 3.1 叢集[Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.1][hdp-2-1-1]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1677">HDInsight 3.1 clusters created before 11/7/2014 were based on hello [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.1][hdp-2-1-1]</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1678">HDInsight 3.0 版會使用為基礎的 hello Hadoop 散發[Hortonworks 資料平台 2.0][hdp-2-0-8]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1678">HDInsight version 3.0 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on hello [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.0][hdp-2-0-8].</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="79c73-1679">HDInsight 2.1 版會使用為基礎的 hello Hadoop 散發[Hortonworks 資料平台 1.3][hdp-1-3-0]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79c73-1679">HDInsight version 2.1 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on hello [Hortonworks Data Platform 1.3][hdp-1-3-0].</span></span>
